Enforcement එෙකන්- ඒ අභɕන්තර ෙදපාර්තෙම්න්තුෙවන්- ගාර්දිෙහේවා සරත් චන්දලාල් ෙෆොන්ෙසේකාට නිකුත් කරපු ඒ Green Card එකට අදාළ ෙල්ඛනය. ඒෙක්ත් එතුමාෙග් ලිපිනය හැටියට දමලා තිෙබන්ෙන් ෙම් සමාගම තිබුණු ෙගදර ලිපිනයමයි. ෙම්ක මම "උ" යනුෙවන් ලකුණු කර සභාගත* කරනවා. ෙම් බලන්න, ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, බඩුත් එක්ක ෙහොරු දැන් අහු ෙවලා. බිමල් රත්නායක ලජ්ජා නැතුව, මහ ෙලොකුවට පාරදෘශɕභාවය ගැන කථා කරනවා; දූෂණය නැති කරන්න ඕනෑ කියලා කථා කරනවා. දූෂිතයන්ට, දූෂණයට හවුල් වුණු අයට -පවුල් වාදය තිෙබන්ෙන් රාජපක්ෂ පවුෙල් ෙනොෙවයි, ෙෆොන්ෙසේකා පවුෙල්.- සතයක්වත් ගිහිල්ලා නැහැයි කියලා කියනවා. මම ෙපන්වන්නම්. ෙමන්න මා ළඟ තිෙබනවා, British Borneo Defence ආයතනය මඟින් ඉදිරිපත් කරන ලද Pro forma Invoices 04ක්. එකක් යූඑස් ෙඩොලර්ස් 134,667යි. Name of the Bank : Bank of America. ඊ ළඟට, Beneficiary Account Name: British Borneo Defence. එතෙකොට ෙම් අය කියනවා, ලංකාෙව් තිෙබන, අර මුලින් කියපු සමාගම HICORP (Pvt.) Limited - HICORP (Pvt.) Limited තමයි ෙම් ෙගොල්ලන් ෙම්වා වහ ගන්න හදාපු සමාගම. ෙම්වා වහ ගන්න බෑනා හැදුවා සමාගමක්, තමන්ෙග් මිතයන් කීප ෙදනකු දාලා. නමුත් වැරැදුණා එක ෙදයක්. මුදල් ගිෙය් HICORP (Pvt.) Limited කියන ලංකාෙව් සමාගමට ෙනොෙවයි; British Borneo Defence කියන ඕස්ෙට්ලියානු සමාගමට ෙනොෙවයි. බෑනාෙග් සමාගමට. මම "ඌ" වශෙයන් ලකුණු කර සභාගත* කරනවා, බෑනාෙග් ඒ සමාගමට මුදල් ගිය Invoices හතරක්.

ගරු ආචාර්ය මර්වින් සිල්වා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு கலாநிதி ேமர்வின் சில்வா) (The Hon. (Dr.) Mervyn Silva) කැත මිනිෙහක් ෙන්. ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா) (The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva) ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ෙමන්න බිමල් රත්නායක මන්තීතුමාට උත්තරය. බෑනාෙග් ඇෙමරිකාෙව් සමාගමට සල්ලි ගිය invoices. ෙමතැන account number එක තිෙබනවා. බෑනාටයි සල්ලි ගිහිල්ලා තිෙබන්ෙන්. ලංකාෙව් ෙනොදන්නා ෙමොකක්ෙදෝ සමාගමක් ෙම් business එක කළා කියලා බිමල් රත්නායක මන්තීතුමා කියනවා. [මූලාසනෙය් අණ පරිදි ඉවත් කරන ලදී.] [அக்கிராசனக் கட்டைளப்பᾊ அகற்றப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ] [Expunged on the order of the Chair.] එතුමාට. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, කන්න ඕනෑ වුණාම කබර ෙගොයාත් තල ෙගොයා ෙවලා ජනතා විමුක්ති ෙපරමුණට. අද අෙප් අතිගරු ජනාධිපතිතුමාට පහර ගහනවා කිසිම පදනමක් නැතුව. ෙම් ෙල්ඛනවලින් අද බඩුත් එක්ක ෙහොරු අහු ෙවලා තිෙබනවා. ෙම් ෙල්ඛන අසතɕ ඒවා බවට කියන්න පුළුවන්කමක් නැහැ. ෙම් ෙල්ඛන ඔස්ෙසේ අපි ඉල්ලීමක් කර සිටිනවා රජෙයන්. ෙම් ගැන පරීක්ෂණයක් පවත්වන්නට ඕනෑ. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, ෙමොකද එතුමාට කිසිම සදාචාරාත්මක අයිතියක් නැහැ, යුද හමුදාෙව් නායකයා වශෙයන් එවැනි ෙදයක් කරන්න. එතුමාම ගිහින් කිව්වා, "දූෂණය වළක්වන්න මම ෙටන්ඩර් මණ්ඩලෙය් හිටියා" කියලා. හැබැයි මම ඉදිරිපත් කරනවා, තවත් ෙල්ඛනයක් ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි. දූෂණ වළක්වන්න කියලා ෙටන්ඩර් මණ්ඩලෙය් හිටියාට එතුමා ෙටන්ඩර් දීලා තිෙබන්ෙන් ෙම්

ආකාරෙයන් සිය බෑනාට සම්බන්ධකම් පවත්වන ෙම් සමාගමට. මීට වඩා අඩුෙවන් සමහර ෙටන්ඩර් දාලා තිබුණා. ඒ ෙටන්ඩර් ඉවත් කරලා. නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, කථාව අවසාන කරන්න. ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா) (The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva) තව විනාඩි ෙදකක් ෙදන්න ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි. ගරු ආචාර්ය මර්වින් සිල්වා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு கலாநிதி ேமர்வின் சில்வா) (The Hon. (Dr.) Mervyn Silva) ෙම්ක මහා ෙහොරකමක් ෙන්. බෑනාෙග් වැඩක්. ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா) (The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva) ඒ ෙටන්ඩර් ඉවත් කරලා තීන්දු දුන්නා, තමන්ෙග් බෑනාෙග් සමාගමට. ඒ විතරක් ෙනොෙවයි. ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, බෑනා ෙමොනවාද කරන්ෙන් කියලා දුව ෙදන්න ඉස්ෙසල්ලා මාමා දන්ෙන් නැද්ද? ෙමොන business ද කරන්ෙන් කියලා දන්ෙන් නැද්ද? සාමානɕෙයන් දරුවකු දීග ෙදන ෙකොට අපි අහනවා, "ෙමොනවාද කරන්ෙන්, ෙගවල් ෙදොරවල් තිෙබනවාද, ෙමොකක්ද කරන business එක?" කියලා. ඉතින් ෙෆොන්ෙසේකා මැතිතුමා ෙම්වා දන්ෙන් නැතුවද හිටිෙය්? එතුමා එෙහම ෙපොඩි බෙබක් ෙනොෙවයි. ෙම් සියල්ල දැන ෙගන ඔහුම ෙටන්ඩර් මණ්ඩලෙය් වාඩි ෙවලා, ෙම් විධියට බෑනාෙග් සමාගමට ඒවා දීලා තිෙබනවා. සදාචාරාත්මකවම ඒක වැරැදියි ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි. ෙම්ක අපට පශ්නයක් ෙවලායි තිෙබන්ෙන්. නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ගරු ඇමතිතුමනි, ෙමොෙහොතක් නිශ්ශබ්ද වන්න. සභාෙව් කටයුතු විනාඩි තුනකින් දීර්ඝ කිරීම සඳහා සභාෙව් අවසරය පතනවා. ගරු මන්තීවරු (மாண்ᾗமிகு உᾠப்பினர்கள்) (Hon. Members)

Aye. ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு நிமல் சிறிபால த சில்வா) (The Hon. Nimal Siripala de Silva) ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි, අෙනක් අයෙග් දූෂණ වළක්වන්න, ඒ ගැන ෙහොයන්න, යහ පාලනයක් ඇති කරන්න එනවාය කියන පුද්ගලයාෙග් කියා කලාපෙයන් බිඳක් තමයි ෙම්. තව ඉදිරියට තව තව ෙද්වල් ෙහොයා ගන්න පුළුවන් ෙව්වි. ෙහොඳ ෙහොඳ ඒවා එළි ෙවන ජාමයට ලු. ඒ වාෙග් තව ටික කාලයක් යන ෙකොට ෙම් පිළිබඳව පරීක්ෂණ පවත්වලා - ගහපු ෙහොර අත්සන් පිළිබඳව දැන් ඇෙමරිකාෙව් පරීක්ෂණ පැවැත්ෙවනවා. ෙහොර අත්සන් ගැහුවා කියලා බෑනාට විරුද්ධව යම් යම් ෙචෝදනා පිළිබඳව දැනටමත් ඇෙමරිකාෙව් පරීක්ෂණ පවත්වනවා ගරු නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමනි. ඒ නිසා අපි කියනවා, ෙමන්න ෙමය. ජනතා විමුක්ති ෙපරමුණට- මම හිතන්ෙන් එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂය ෙම් ගැන කථා කරන්ෙන් නැහැ කියලායි. ෙමොකද, එක්සත් ජාතික පක්ෂයට ෙම් ගැන කථා කරන්න බැහැ.- ෛදවෙය් සරදම තමයි සිද්ධ ෙවලා තිෙබන්ෙන්. ෙමවැනි අෙප්ක්ෂකෙයක් කෙර් තියා ෙගන ගිහිල්ලා දූෂණය නැති කරන්නට කථා කිරීම ෙම් යුගෙය්

* පුස්තකාලෙය් තබා ඇත. ᾓனிைலயத்தில் ைவக்கப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ. Placed in the Library.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2005 2006

ෙලොකුම විහිළුව බව පකාශ කරමින්, ෙමවැනි පුද්ගලයන්ට ජනවාරි මාසෙය් 26 වන දා ෙම් රෙට් ජනතාව නිසි පිළිතුරු ෙදන බව පකාශ කරමින් මෙග් කථාව අවසන් කරනවා. සභාෙම්සය මත තබන ලද ලියවිල්ල : சபாபீடத்தில் ைவக்கப்பட்ட ஆவணம் : Document tabled:

පශ්නය විමසන ලදී. කටහඬවල් අනුව "පක්ෂ" මන්තීන්ට ජය බව නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා විසින් පකාශ කරන ලදී.

வினா விᾌக்கப்பட்டᾐ. குரல்களின்பᾊ, "ஆம்"ேமேலாங்கிற்ᾠ என பிரதிச்சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள் அறிவித்தார்கள். Question put. MR. DEPUTY SPEAKER , having collected the Voices, declared that the “Ayes" had it.

ගරු ආර්. සම්පන්දන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஆர். சம்பந்தன்) (The Hon. R. Sampanthan)

Divide! පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 43 වන ස්ථාවර නිෙයෝගය යටෙත් - පක්ෂව 97: විරුද්ධව 18 යනුෙවන් - ෙබදුෙණ්ය.

பாராᾦமன்றம் 43 ஆம் நிைலக் கட்டைளப்பᾊ பிாிந்தᾐ:

சார்பாக 97; எதிராக 18. The Parliament divided under Standing Order No. 43: Ayes 97 ;

Noes 18 . නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා (பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள்) (The Deputy Speaker) ඒ අනුව ෙයෝජනාව වැඩි ඡන්දෙයන් සම්මත වූ බව මම පකාශ කරමි.

කල්තැබීම

ஒத்திைவப்ᾗ ADJOURNMENT එකල්හි ෙව්ලාව අ. භා. 4.00 පසු කර තිබුෙණන් නිෙයෝජɕ කථානායකතුමා විසින් පශ්නය ෙනොවිමසා පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව කල් තබන ලදී. පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව ඊට අනුකූලව, අ. භා. 4.07ට, අද දින සභා සම්මතිය අනුව, 2010 ෙපබරවාරි 05 වන සිකුරාදා පූ. භා. 9.30 වන ෙතක් කල් ගිෙය්ය. அப்ெபாᾨᾐ ேநரம் பி.ப 4.00 மணிக்குப் பிந்திவிட்டைமயால், பிரதிச் சபாநாயகர் அவர்கள் வினா விᾌக்காமேலேய பாராᾦமன்றத்ைத ஒத்திைவத்தார். அதன்பᾊ, பாராᾦமன்றம் பி.ப 4.07க்கு, அதனᾐ இன்ைறய தீர்மானத்திற்கிணங்க, 2010 ெபப்ரவாி 05, ெவள்ளிக்கிழைம ᾙ.ப. 9.30 மணி வைர ஒத்திைவக்கப்பட்டᾐ. And it being past 4.00 p.m., MR. DEPUTY SPEAKER adjourned Parliament without Question put. Adjourned accordingly at 4.07 p.m. until 9.30 a.m.. on Friday, 05th February, 2009, pursuant to the Resolution of Parliament of this Day. පශ්නවලට ලිඛිත පිළිතුරු வினாக்கᾦக்கு எᾨத்ᾐᾚல விைடகள்

WRITTEN ANSWERS TO QUESTIONS අක්මීමණ පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු அக்மீமன பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் AKMEEMANA PRADESHIYA SABHA AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS

0551/’09 1. ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு அஜித் குமார) (The Hon. Ajith Kumara) පළාත් පාලන සහ පළාත් සභා අමාතɕතුමාෙගන් ඇසූ පශ්නය - (2): (අ) (i) අක්මීමණ පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය තුළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් ෙම් වන විට සවි කර තිෙබන දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු සංඛɕාව හා එම ස්ථානයන්හි ලිපිනයන් කවෙර්ද; (ii) අදාළ සමාගම් හා කුලුනු සවි කළ වර්ෂයන් කවෙර්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට දන්වන්ෙනහිද? (ආ) (i) එම කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට අදාළව ඉටු කළ යුතු ෙකොන්ෙද්සි කවෙර්ද; (ii) ෙමහිදී අදාළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් එක් එක් ස්ථාන සඳහා අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා තිෙබ්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට ඉදිරිපත් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඇ) අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා ෙනොමැති විට, දුරකථන කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට පළාත් පාලන ආයතනය අනුමතිය දී ඇත්නම් එය වරදක් බව එතුමා පිළිගන්ෙනහිද? (ඈ) (i) එෙසේ නම් ඒ සම්බන්ධව ගනු ලබන කියා මාර්ගය කවෙර්ද; (ii) කුලුනු සවි කිරීෙම්දී පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ලැබිය යුතු මුදල හා ලැබී ඇති මුදල ෙවන ෙවනම ෙකොපමණද;

[ගරු නිමල් සිරිපාල ද සිල්වා මහතා]

2010 ජනවාරි 05 2007 2008

(iii) අදාළ මුදල් ලැබී ෙනොමැති නම් ඒ සම්බන්ධෙයන් ගනු ලබන කියාමාර්ගය කවෙර්ද; (iv) පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ෙමෙතක් ලැබී ඇති ඉහත මුදල් වැය කර ඇත්ෙත් කවර කටයුතු සඳහා ද; යන්න එතුමා සඳහන් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඉ) ෙනොඑෙසේ නම් ඒ මන්ද?

உள்ᾧராட்சி, மாகாணசைபகள் அைமச்சைரக் ேகட்ட வினா: (அ)(i ) அக்மீமன பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசத்தில் ெதாைலேபசி கம்பனிகளால் தற்ேபாᾐ ெபாᾞத்தப்பட்ᾌள்ள ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்களின் எண்ணிக்ைக மற்ᾠம் அந்த இடங்களின் ᾙகவாிகள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) உாிய கம்பனிகᾦம் வᾞடᾙம் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா? (ஆ) (i ) இந்த கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்குாியதாக ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யேவண்ᾊய நிபந்தைனகள் யாைவ ெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) இதன்ேபாᾐ உாிய ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பனிகள், ஒவ்ெவாᾞ இடத்திற்கும் தனித்தனியாக உாிய நிபந்தைனகைள ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்ᾐள்ளனவா என்பைதᾜம்

அவர் இச்சைபக்குச் சமர்ப்பிப்பாரா?

(இ) உாிய நிபந்தைனகள் ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யப்படாத நிைலயில், ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்கு உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனம் அங்கீகாரம் வழங்கி யிᾞந்தால் அᾐ ஒᾞ குற்றமாகும் என்பைத அவர் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்வாரா? (ஈ)(i ) ஆெமனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐம்ேபாᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடக்க ேவண்ᾊய பணᾙம் கிைடத்ᾐள்ள பணᾙம் ெவவ்ேவறாக எவ்வள ெவன்பைதᾜம், (iii ) உாிய பணத்ெதாைக கிைடக்கவில்ைலெயனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i v ) உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடத்த ேமற்பᾊ பணத்ெதாைக எந்த நடவᾊக்ைககᾦக்காக ெசலவிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ என்பைதᾜம் அவர் குறிப்பிᾌவாரா? (உ) இன்ேறல், ஏன்? asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils: (a) Will he inform this House of- (i) the number of telephone communication towers installed by telephone companies in the Akmeemana Pradeshiya Sabha area and the addresses of their locations; and (ii) the relevant companies and the year? (b) Will he submit to this House- (i) the conditions that have to be fulfilled with regard to the installation of these towers; and

(ii) whether the relevant conditions have been fulfilled separately as per each location by the relevant telephone companies? (c) Will he admit that it is an offence, if the local government authority had given permission to install telephone towers when the relevant conditions have not been fulfilled? (d) Will he state- (i) if so, the measures taken in this regard; (ii) separately, the amount of money payable to the local government authority in installing the towers and the amount of money that had been received; (iii) if the relevant money had not been received, the measures that will be taken in that regard; and (iv) the purposes for which the above money received by the local government authority had been spent? (iv) After crediting to the common fund of the Local Authority, funds will be utilized for the functions approved under the Annual Budget Statement. (e) Does not arise. 1. Sharing of Antenna Structures 1.1 Antenna structures should be used on sharing basis for which the tariff schedule will be determined by TRCSL in consultation with the TISPs. The minimum number of antenna structures that conform to the technical requirements will be approved for an identified Antenna Structure Farm. 1.2 The TRCSL will initiate the formation of a new Antenna Structure Farm when the necessity arises. TISPs may propose such locations to TRCSL. 1.3 The antenna structure shall be designed and constructed to accommodate a minimum of 20 square meters of additional design antenna area (from the top portion) for at least two other TSPs. Physical space required for fixing of the additional antenna shall be reserved at top portion. This allocation of additional design antenna area will be encouraged through incentive schemes. 1.4 Initially up to three requests will be considered to construct separate antenna structures within the Antenna Structure Farm. Subsequent applicants should share one of the available antenna structures. Applications for additional antenna structures will be considered only under special circumstances and such applications will be referred to the TAC with justification for such request. 1.5 The Antenna Structure Farm will be confined to a minimum feasible area by the TRCSL, subject to a maximum radius of 250 m. 1.6 The distance between Antenna Structure Farms will be kept at a minimum separation of 4 km. 1.7 Both TSPs and TISPs may obtain approval to erect roof top masts of height not exceeding 20 meters from the roof top within or in between Antenna Structure Farms. 1.8 Broadcasting antenna structures are exempted from the clauses 1.3 and 1.4 provided that application is initially forwarded for an Antenna Structure to be used only for broadcasting purposes.

[ගරු ජනක බණ්ඩාර ෙතන්නෙකෝන් මහතා]

2010 ජනවාරි 05 2011 2012

1.9 Cumulative radio frequency power density due to Antenna Structure Farm should be within the limits defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL provided that the maximum RF power levels allowed are as per Annexure I. 2. Height Clearance 2.1 Maximum height of the antenna structure shall be based on the recommendations of the CAASL, MOD and UDA. 3. Lightning Protection 3.1 The Antenna Structure premises should be provided with a comprehensive lightning protection scheme to minimize the lightning related damage and injury as per the Annexure II (a). 3.2 The antenna structure should conform to the guidelines specified in Annexure II (b) with regard to the lightning protection concerns. 3.3 installation of the lightning protection system should be carried out by the TISP as per Annexure II (b). 3.4 An insurance cover shall be in place against any lightning related damage to the neighbourhood due to the existence of the antenna structure. 3.5 A report on the lighting protection system, and other specified information as per Annexure III, shall be submitted to TRCSL by TISP twice a year. 4. Electromagnetic Interference and Health Concerns 4.1 Base Station equipment shall comply with the EMC standards acceptable to TRCSL. 4.2 TRCSL will enforce and monitor maximum RF power density criteria defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL as per Annexure I. 4.3 Verification of compliance with stipulated standards will be carried out by TRCSL or a recognized institution to ensure public safety. 5. Environmental Concerns 5.1 Natural environment of the area shall be protected from any potential adverse impacts in accordance with CEA or PEA approval. 6. Construction of Antenna Structures 6.1 The Antenna structure and other related infrastructure should be designed and constructed in conformity with BS 8100, TIA/EIA 222F (or latest) or other equivalent international standard accepted by TRCSL. 6.2 All antenna structures with heights exceeding 30m should be designed and detailed as post - disaster type structures. 6.3 All the structural designs, construction drawings and proposals are required to be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 6.4 Institutes and individuals who do the certification should be registered with TRC. 6.5 Minimum of third-party insurance coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury should be taken during the construction of antenna structure. A copy of the same should be submitted to TRCSL before commencement of the development. 6.6 During the construction, the antenna structure should be installed with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations.

6.7 TISPs should obtain development permits from respective Local Authorities. All the approving agencies are encouraged to establish electronic document transfer in order to expedite the approval process. 6.8 TISP who has received approval is required to complete the construction of the new antenna structure within six months from the date of granting the approval. Failure to meet this requirement without a valid reason acceptable to TRCSL will result in cancellation of the approval. The new antenna structure should be available for sharing within 03 months from the date of completion. 6.9 No Telecommunication Antenna Structure should be constructed without written approval of TRCSL. 7. Installation of Antenna Structures on Buildings 7.1 The structural stability of the buildings, which are primarily designed for purposes other than facilitating antenna structures, should be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design, prior to the approval for the construction of the Antenna Structure. 7.2 The TISP should obtain the planning clearance from UDA within the areas declared under UDA Low. 7.3 Antenna structure outside the areas declared under UDA Law will be considered for approval with the consent of relevant Local Authorities. 7.4 Antenna structures less than 5m in height above roof top level are required to obtain clearance only from the MOD and CAASL. 7.5 A lightning protection system should be installed as per the Annexure II (b), to ensure the safety of occupants. 7.6 All antenna structures on buildings with total height exceeding 30m above ground level should be designed and detailed as post-disaster type structures. All proposals shall be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 7.7 Installations of Antenna Structures on buildings should conform to all other Guidelines in this document. 8. Maintenance of Antenna Structures 8.1 Lighting and painting of Antenna Structures must be in accordance with the specifications of CAASL. 8.2 Antenna structure operator should submit a monthly report in electronic form to TRCSL indicating the information as per format No: TRC/NWMR - 01. 8.3 Maintenance of antenna structure shall be carried out in accordance with Annexure IV. 8.4 Maintenance of Lightning protection system should be done by the TISP in compliance with specifications given in Annexure II (c).. 9. Alteration to Antenna Structures 9.1 Upon justifiable request(s) made by concerned parties, the TRCSL, in consultation with relevant authorities, may consider removal or alteration to the structure or suspension of operation. In such case all costs should be borne by the TISP. 9.2 To ensure the safety of the public and property, an Antenna Structure should not be abandoned even for short periods of time, unless otherwise it is completely removed. The TISP should inform the TRCSL and make arrangements to either remove a non-operational installation or transfer it to another

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2013 2014

antennae structure operator. Until the antenna structure is removed or transferred and the TRCSL is informed the same, the TISP is responsible for the maintenance of the antenna structure in conformity with provisions specified. 9.3 Any structural alterations to the Antenna Structure or its supporting structure, beyond what has been envisaged in the approved design, require the certification of a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design to get the approval of the TRCSL. 9.4 Removal of an Antenna Structure also requires insurance to be taken for the coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury during the removal of antenna structure. 10. Approval Procedure 10.1 TISP should submit an application as per Annexure V in the form of soft and hard copies 10.2 Approval Procedure is as specified in Annexure VI. 11. General 11.1 All relevant authorities such as CEA, PEA, UDA, CAASL, LA, CEB and TRCSL are required to facilitate the TISPs in establishing antenna structures to provide telecommunication services on a priority basis, as telecommunication networks are a vital component of infrastructure development while addressing the public health & safety, economic, environmental and other impacts. 11.2 Appeals for any deviation from these guidelines caused by technical or commercial issues will be referred to the TAC who will meet once in a month.

ෙබෝෙප් - ෙපෝද්දල පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු ேபாப்ேப - ேபாத்தல பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் BOPE-PODDALA PRADESHIYA SABHA AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS 0552/’09 2. ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு அஜித் குமார) (The Hon. Ajith Kumara) පළාත් පාලන සහ පළාත් සභා අමාතɕතුමාෙගන් ඇසූ පශ්නය - (2) : (අ) (i) ෙබෝෙප් - ෙපෝද්දල පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය තුල දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් ෙම් වන විට සවි කර තිෙබන දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු සංඛɕාව හා එම ස්ථානයන්හි ලිපිනයන් කවෙර්ද; (ii) අදාළ සමාගම් හා කුලුනු සවි කළ වර්ෂයන් කවෙර්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට දන්වන්ෙනහිද? (ආ) (i) එම කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට අදාළව ඉටු කළ යුතු ෙකොන්ෙද්සි කවෙර්ද; (ii) ෙමහිදී, අදාළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් එක් එක් ස්ථාන සඳහා අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා තිෙබ්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට ඉදිරිපත් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඉ) ෙනොඑෙසේ නම් ඒ මන්ද? உள்ᾧராட்சி, மாகாணசைபகள் அைமச்சைரக் ேகட்ட வினா : (அ) (i) ேபாப்ேப - ேபாத்தல பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசத்தில் ெதாைலேபசி கம்பனிகளால் தற்ேபாᾐ ெபாᾞத்தப்பட்ᾌள்ள ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்களின் எண்ணிக்ைக மற்ᾠம் அந்த இடங்களின் ᾙகவாிகள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், (ii) உாிய கம்பனிகᾦம் வᾞடᾙம் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா? (ஆ) (i) இந்தக் கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்குாியதாக ᾘர்த்திெசய்யேவண்ᾊய நிபந்தைனகள் யாைவ ெயன்பைதᾜம், (ii) இதன்ேபாᾐ உாிய ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பனிகள், ஒவ்ெவாᾞ இடத்திற்கும் தனித்தனியாக உாிய நிபந்தைனகைள ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்ᾐள்ளனவா என்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்குச் சமர்ப்பிப்பாரா? (ஈ) (i) ஆெமனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவ ெயன்பைதᾜம், (ii) கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐம்ேபாᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடக்க ேவண்ᾊய பணᾙம் கிைடத்ᾐள்ள பணᾙம் ெவவ்ேவறாக எவ்வள ெவன்பைதᾜம், (iii) உாிய பணத்ெதாைக கிைடக்கவில்ைலெயனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், (iv) உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடத்த ேமற்பᾊ பணத்ெதாைக எந்த நடவᾊக்ைககᾦக்காக ெசலவிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ என்பைதᾜம் அவர் குறிப்பிᾌவாரா? ඇමුණුම 01 இைணப்ᾗ 01 Annex 01 1.Sharing of Antenna Structures 1.1 Antenna structures should be used on sharing basis for which the tariff schedule will be determined by TRCSL in consultation with the TISPs. The minimum number of antenna structures that conform to the technical requirements will be approved for an identified Antenna Structure Farm. 1.2 The TRCSL will initiate the formation of a new Antenna Structure Farm when the necessity arises. TISPs may propose such locations to TRCSL. 1.3 The antenna structure shall be designed and constructed to accommodate a minimum of 20 square meters of additional design antenna area (from the top portion) for at least two other TSPs. Physical space required for fixing of the additional antenna shall be reserved at top portion. This allocation of additional design antenna area will be encouraged through incentive schemes. 1.4 Initially up to three requests will be considered to construct separate antenna structures within the Antenna Structure Farm. Subsequent applicants should share one of the available antenna structures. Applications for additional antenna structures will be considered only under special circumstances and such applications will be referred to the TAC with justification for such request.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2017 2018

1.5 The Antenna Structure Farm will be confined to a minimum feasible area by the TRCSL, subject to a maximum radius of 250 m. 1.6 The distance between Antenna Structure Farms will be kept at a minimum separation of 4 km. 1.7 Both TSPs and TISPs may obtain approval to erect roof top masts of height not exceeding 20 meters from the roof top within or in between Antenna Structure Farms. 1.8 Broadcasting antenna structures are exempted from the clauses 1.3 and 1.4 provided that application is initially forwarded for an Antenna Structure to be used only for broadcasting purposes. 1.9 Cumulative radio frequency power density due to Antenna Structure Farm should be within the limits defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL provided that the maximum RF power levels allowed are as per Annexure I. 2.Height Clearance 2.1 Maximum height of the antenna structure shall be based on the recommendations of the CAASL, MOD and UDA. 3.Lightning Protection 3.1 The Antenna Structure premises should be provided with a comprehensive lightning protection scheme to minimize the lightning related damage and injury as per the Annexure II (a). 3.2 The antenna structure should conform to the guidelines specified in Annexure II (b) with regard to the lightning protection concerns. 3.3 installation of the lightning protection system should be carried out by the TISP as per Annexure II (b). 3.4 An insurance cover shall be in place against any lightning related damage to the neighbourhood due to the existence of the antenna structure. 3.5 A report on the lighting protection system, and other specified information as per Annexure III, shall be submitted to TRCSL by TISP twice a year. 4.Electromagnetic Interference and Health Concerns 4.1 Base Station equipment shall comply with the EMC standards acceptable to TRCSL. 4.2 TRCSL will enforce and monitor maximum RF power density criteria defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL as per Annexure I. 4.3 Verification of compliance with stipulated standards will be carried out by TRCSL or a recognized institution to ensure public safety. 5.Environmental Concerns

5.1 Natural environment of the area shall be protected from any potential adverse impacts in accordance with CEA or PEA approval. 6.Construction of Antenna Structures 6.1 The Antenna structure and other related infrastructure should be designed and constructed in conformity with BS 8100, TIA/EIA 222F (or latest) or other equivalent international standard accepted by TRCSL. 6.2 All antenna structures with heights exceeding 30m should be designed and detailed as post - disaster type structures. 6.3 All the structural designs, construction drawings and proposals are required to be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 6.4 Institutes and individuals who do the certification should be registered with TRC. 6.5 Minimum of third-party insurance coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury should be taken during the

construction of antenna structure. A copy of the same should be submitted to TRCSL before commencement of the development. 6.6 During the construction, the antenna structure should be installed with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 6.7 TISPs should obtain development permits from respective Local Authorities. All the approving agencies are encouraged to establish electronic document transfer in order to expedite the approval process. 6.8 TISP who has received approval is required to complete the construction of the new antenna structure within six months from the date of granting the approval. Failure to meet this requirement without a valid reason acceptable to TRCSL will result in cancellation of the approval. The new antenna structure should be available for sharing within 03 months from the date of completion. 6.9 No Telecommunication Antenna Structure should be constructed without written approval of TRCSL. 7.Installation of Antenna Structures on Buildings 7.1 The structural stability of the buildings, which are primarily designed for purposes other than facilitating antenna structures, should be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design, prior to the approval for the construction of the Antenna Structure. 7.2 The TISP should obtain the planning clearance from UDA with in the areas declared under UDA Law. 7.3 Antenna structure outside the areas declared under UDA Law will be considered for approval with the consent of relevant Local Authorities. 7.4 Antenna structures less than 5m in height above roof top level are required to obtain clearance only from the MOD and CAASL. 7.5 A lightning protection system should be installed as per the Annexure II (b), to ensure the safety of occupants. 7.6 All antenna structures on buildings with total height exceeding 30m above ground level should be designed and detailed as post-disaster type structures. All proposals shall be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 7.7 Installations of Antenna Structures on buildings should conform to all other Guidelines in this document. 8.Maintenance of Antenna Structures

8.1 Lighting and painting of Antenna Structures must be in accordance with the specifications of CAASL. 8.2 Antenna structure operator should submit a monthly report in electronic form to TRCSL indicating the information as per format No: TRC/NWMR - 01. 8.3 Maintenance of antenna structure shall be carried out in accordance with Annexure IV. 8.4 Maintenance of Lightning protection system should be done by the TISP in compliance with specifications given in Annexure II (c).. 9.Alteration to Antenna Structures 9.1 Upon justifiable request(s) made by concerned parties, the TRCSL, in consultation with relevant authorities, may consider removal or alteration to the structure or suspension of operation. In such see all costs should be borne by the TISP. 9.2 To ensure the safety of the public and property, an Antenna Structure should not be abandoned even for short periods of

[ගරු ජනක බණ්ඩාර ෙතන්නෙකෝන් මහතා]

2010 ජනවාරි 05

time, unless otherwise it is completely removed. The TISP should inform the TRCSL and make arrangements to either remove a non-operational installation or transfer it to another antennae structure operator. Until the antenna structure is removed or transferred and the TRCSL is informed the same, the TISP is responsible for the maintenance of the antenna structure in conformity with provisions specified. 9.3 Any structural alterations to the Antenna Structure or its supporting structure, beyond what has been envisaged in the approved design, require the certification of a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design to get the approval of the TRCSL. 9.4 Removal of an Antenna Structure also requires insurance to be taken for the coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury during the removal of antenna structure. 10.Approval Procedure 10.1 TISP should submit an application as per Annexure V in the form of soft and hard copies. 10.2 Approval Procedure is as specified in Annexure VI. 11.General 11.1 All relevant authorities such as CEA, PEA, UDA, CAASL, LA, CEB and TRCSL are required to facilitate the TISPs in establishing antenna structures to provide telecommunication services on a priority basis, as telecommunication networks are a vital component of infrastructure development while addressing the public health & safety, economic, environmental and other impacts. 11.2 Appeals for any deviation from these guidelines caused by technical or commercial issues will be referred to the TAC who will meet once in a month.

හික්කඩුව නගර සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු ஹிக்கᾌவ நகர சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் HIKKADUWA URBAN COUNCIL AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS

0553/’09 3. ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு அஜித் குமார) (The Hon. Ajith Kumara) පළාත් පාලන සහ පළාත් සභා අමාතɕතුමාෙගන් ඇසූ පශ්නය - (2) : (අ) (i) හික්කඩුව නගර සභා බල පෙද්ශය තුළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් ෙම් වන විට සවි කර තිෙබන දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු සංඛɕාව හා එම ස්ථානයන්හි ලිපිනයන් කවෙර්ද; (ii) අදාළ සමාගම් හා කුලුනු සවි කළ වර්ෂයන් කවෙර්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට දන්වන්ෙනහිද? (ආ) (i) එම කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට අදාළව ඉටු කළ යුතු ෙකොන්ෙද්සි කවෙර්ද; (ii) ෙමහිදී, අදාළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් එක් එක් ස්ථාන සඳහා අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා තිෙබ්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට ඉදිරිපත් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඇ) අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා ෙනොමැති විට, දුරකථන කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට පළාත් පාලන ආයතනය අනුමතිය දී ඇත්නම් එය වරදක් බව එතුමා පිළිගන්ෙනහිද? (ඈ) (i) එෙසේ නම් ඒ සම්බන්ධව ගනු ලබන කියා මාර්ගය කවෙර්ද; (ii) කුලුනු සවි කිරීෙම්දී පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ලැබිය යුතු මුදල හා ලැබී ඇති මුදල ෙවන ෙවනම ෙකොපමණද;

(iii) අදාළ මුදල් ලැබී ෙනොමැති නම් ඒ සම්බන්ධෙයන් ගනු ලබන කියාමාර්ගය කවෙර්ද; (iv) පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ෙමෙතක් ලැබී ඇති ඉහත මුදල් වැය කර ඇත්ෙත් කවර කටයුතු සඳහා ද; යන්න එතුමා සඳහන් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඉ) ෙනොඑෙසේ නම් ඒ මන්ද? உள்ᾧராட்சி, மாகாணசைபகள் அைமச்சைரக் ேகட்ட வினா: (அ) (i) ஹிக்கᾌவ நகர சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசத்தில் ெதாைலேபசி கம்பனிகளால் தற்ேபாᾐ ெபாᾞத்தப் பட்ᾌள்ள ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்களின் எண்ணிக்ைக மற்ᾠம் அந்த இடங்களின் ᾙகவாிகள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், (ii) உாிய கம்பனிகᾦம் வᾞடᾙம் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா? (ஆ) (i) இந்த கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்குாியதாக ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யேவண்ᾊய நிபந்தைனகள் யாைவெயன்ப ைதᾜம், (ii) இதன்ேபாᾐ உாிய ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பனிகள், ஒவ்ெவாᾞ இடத்திற்கும் தனித்தனியாக உாிய நிபந்தைனகைள ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்ᾐள்ளனவா என்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்குச் சமர்ப்பிப்பாரா? (இ) உாிய நிபந்தைனகள் ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யப்படாத நிைலயில், ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்கு உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனம் அங்கீகாரம் வழங்கியிᾞந்தால் அᾐ ஒᾞ குற்றமாகும் என்பைத அவர் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்வாரா? (ஈ) (i) ஆெமனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவ ெயன்பைதᾜம், (ii) கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐம்ேபாᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடக்க ேவண்ᾊய பணᾙம் கிைடத்ᾐள்ள பணᾙம் ெவவ்ேவறாக எவ்வள ெவன்பைதᾜம், (iii) உாிய பணத்ெதாைக கிைடக்கவில்ைலெயனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், (iv) உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடத்த ேமற்பᾊ பணத்ெதாைக எந்த நடவᾊக்ைககᾦக்காக ெசலவிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ என்பைதᾜம் அவர் குறிப்பிᾌவாரா? (உ) இன்ேறல், ஏன்?

asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils: (a) Will he inform this House of- (i) the number of telephone communication towers installed by telephone companies in the Hikkaduwa Urban Council area and the addresses of their locations; and (ii) the relevant companies and the year? (b) Will he submit to this House- (i) the conditions that have to be fulfilled with regard to the installation of these towers; and (ii) whether the relevant conditions have been fulfilled separately as per each location by the relevant telephone companies?

(e) If not, why?

(ஆ) (i) ெதாைலத்ெதாடர்ᾗகள் ஒᾨங்குபᾌத்தல் ஆைணக் குᾨவினால் விதிக்கப்பட்ᾌள்ள நிபந்தைனகள் இைணப்ᾗ இல்கம் 01 இல குறிப்பிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளன. (i) ஆம் (இ) ஆம் (ஈ) (i) அவ்வாறான சந்தர்ப்பங்கள் ெதாியவᾞமாயின் குறித்த சட்ட ஏற்பாᾌகᾦக்கு அைமய நடவᾊக்ைக ேமற்ெகாள்ளப்பᾌம். (e) Does not arise. ඇමුණුම 01 இைணப்ᾗ 01 Annex 01 1. Sharing of Antenna Structures 1.1 Antenna structures should be used on sharing basis for which the tariff schedule will be determined by TRCSL in consultation with the TISPs. The minimum number of antenna structures that conform to the technical requirements will be approved for an identified Antenna Structure Farm. 1.2 The TRCSL will initiate the formation of a new Antenna Structure Farm when the necessity arises. TISPs may propose such locations to TRCSL. 1.3 The antenna structure shall be designed and constructed to accommodate a minimum of 20 square meters of additional design antenna area (from the top portion) for at least two other TSPs. Physical space required for fixing of the additional antenna shall be reserved at top portion. This allocation of additional design antenna area will be encouraged through incentive schemes.

[ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා]

2010 ජනවාරි 05 2023 2024

1.4 Initially up to three requests will be considered to construct separate antenna structures within the Antenna Structure Farm. Subsequent applicants should share one of the available antenna structures. Applications for additional antenna structures will be considered only under special circumstances and such applications will be referred to the TAC with justification for such request. 1.5 The Antenna Structure Farm will be confined to a minimum feasible area by the TRCSL, subject to a maximum radius of 250 m. 1.6 The distance between Antenna Structure Farms will be kept at a minimum separation of 4 km. 1.7 Both TSPs and TISPs may obtain approval to erect roof top masts of height not exceeding 20 meters from the roof top within or in between Antenna Structure Farms. 1.8 Broadcasting antenna structures are exempted from the clauses 1.3 and 1.4 provided that application is initially forwarded for an Antenna Structure to be used only for broadcasting purposes. 1.9 Cumulative radio frequency power density due to Antenna Structure Farm should be within the limits defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL provided that the maximum RF power levels allowed are as per Annexure I. 2. Height Clearance 2.1 Maximum height of the antenna structure shall be based on the recommendations of the CAASL, MOD and UDA. 3. Lightning Protection 3.1 The Antenna Structure premises should be provided with a comprehensive lightning protection scheme to minimize the lightning related damage and injury as per the Annexure II (a). 3.2 The antenna structure should conform to the guidelines specified in Annexure II (b) with regard to the lightning protection concerns. 3.3 installation of the lightning protection system should be carried out by the TISP as per Annexure II (b). 3.4 An insurance cover shall be in place against any lightning related damage to the neighbourhood due to the existence of the antenna structure. 3.5 A report on the lighting protection system, and other specified information as per Annexure III, shall be submitted to TRCSL by TISP twice a year. 4. Electromagnetic Interference and Health Concerns 4.1 Base Station equipment shall comply with the EMC standards acceptable to TRCSL. 4.2 TRCSL will enforce and monitor maximum RF power density criteria defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL as per Annexure I. 4.3 Verification of compliance with stipulated standards will be carried out by TRCSL or a recognized institution to ensure public safety. 5. Environmental Concerns 5.1 Natural environment of the area shall be protected from any potential adverse impacts in accordance with CEA or PEA approval. 6. Construction of Antenna Structures 6.1 The Antenna structure and other related infrastructure should be designed and constructed in conformity with BS 8100, TIA/EIA 222F (or latest) or other equivalent international standard accepted by TRCSL. 6.2 All antenna structures with heights exceeding 30m should be designed and detailed as post - disaster type structures. 6.3 All the structural designs, construction drawings and proposals are required to be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 6.4 Institutes and individuals who do the certification should be registered with TRC.

6.5 Minimum of third-party insurance coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury should be taken during the construction of antenna structure. A copy of the same should be submitted to TRCSL before commencement of the development. 6.6 During the construction, the antenna structure should be installed with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 6.7 TISPs should obtain development permits from respective Local Authorities. All the approving agencies are encouraged to establish electronic document transfer in order to expedite the approval process. 6.8 TISP who has received approval is required to complete the construction of the new antenna structure within six months from the date of granting the approval. Failure to meet this requirement without a valid reason acceptable to TRCSL will result in cancellation of the approval. The new antenna structure should be available for sharing within 03 months from the date of completion. 6.9 No Telecommunication Antenna Structure should be constructed without written approval of TRCSL. 7. Installation of Antenna Structures on Buildings 7.1 The structural stability of the buildings, which are primarily designed for purposes other than facilitating antenna structures, should be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design, prior to the approval for the construction of the Antenna Structure. 7.2 The TISP should obtain the planning clearance from UDA with the areas declared under UDA Law. 7.3 Antenna structure outside the areas declared under UDA Law will be considered for approval with the consent of relevant Local Authorities. 7.4 Antenna structures less than 5m in height above roof top level are required to obtain clearance only from the MOD and CAASL. 7.5 A lightning protection system should be installed as per the Annexure II (b), to ensure the safety of occupants. 7.6 All antenna structures on buildings with total height exceeding 30m above ground level should be designed and detailed as post-disaster type structures. All proposals shall be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 7.7 Installations of Antenna Structures on buildings should conform to all other Guidelines in this document.

8. Maintenance of Antenna Structures 8.1 Lighting and painting of Antenna Structures must be in accordance with the specifications of CAASL. 8.2 Antenna structure operator should submit a monthly report in electronic form to TRCSL indicating the information as per format No: TRC/NWMR - 01. 8.3 Maintenance of antenna structure shall be carried out in accordance with Annexure IV. 8.4 Maintenance of Lightning protection system should be done by the TISP in compliance with specifications given in Annexure II (c).. 9. Alteration to Antenna Structures 9.1 Upon justifiable request(s) made by concerned parties, the TRCSL, in consultation with relevant authorities, may consider removal or alteration to the structure or suspension of operation. In such case all costs should be borne by the TISP. 9.2 To ensure the safety of the public and property, an Antenna Structure should not be abandoned even for short periods of time, unless otherwise it is completely removed. The TISP should inform the TRCSL and make arrangements to either remove a non-operational installation or transfer it to another antenna structure operator. Until the antenna structure is removed or transferred and the TRCSL is informed the same, the TISP is responsible for the maintenance of the antenna structure in conformity with provisions specified.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2025 2026

9.3 Any structural alterations to the Antenna Structure or its supporting structure, beyond what has been envisaged in the approved design, require the certification of a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design to get the approval of the TRCSL. 9.4 Removal of an Antenna Structure also requires insurance to be taken for the coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury during the removal of antenna structure. 10. Approval Procedure 10.1 TISP should submit an application as per Annexure V in the form of soft and hard copies. 10.2 Approval Procedure is as specified in Annexure VI. 11. General 11.1 All relevant authorities such as CEA, PEA, UDA, CAASL, LA, CEB and TRCSL are required to facilitate the TISPs in establishing antenna structures to provide telecommunication services on a priority basis, as telecommunication networks are a vital component of infrastructure development while addressing the public health & safety, economic, environmental and other impacts. 11.2 Appeals for any deviation from these guidelines caused by technical or commercial issues will be referred to the TAC who will meet once in a month.

බද්ෙද්ගම පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු பத்ேதகம பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் BADDEGAMA PRADESHIYA SABHA AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS 0554/’09 4. ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා ( மாண்ᾗமிகு அஜித் குமார) (The Hon. Ajith Kumara) පළාත් පාලන සහ පළාත් සභා අමාතɕතුමාෙගන් ඇසූ පශ්නය - (2) : (අ) (i) බද්ෙද්ගම පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය තුළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් ෙම් වන විට සවි කර තිෙබන දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු සංඛɕාව හා එම ස්ථානයන්හි ලිපිනයන් කවෙර්ද; (ii) අදාළ සමාගම් හා කුලුනු සවි කළ වර්ෂයන් කවෙර්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට දන්වන්ෙනහිද? (ආ) (i) එම කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට අදාළව ඉටු කළ යුතු ෙකොන්ෙද්සි කවෙර්ද; (ii) ෙමහිදී අදාළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් එක් එක් ස්ථාන සඳහා අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා තිෙබ්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට ඉදිරිපත් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඇ) අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා ෙනොමැති විට, දුරකථන කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට පළාත් පාලන ආයතනය අනුමතිය දී ඇත්නම් එය වරදක් බව එතුමා පිළිගන්ෙනහිද? (iv) පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ෙමෙතක් ලැබී ඇති ඉහත මුදල් වැය කර ඇත්ෙත් කවර කටයුතු සඳහා ද; යන්න එතුමා සඳහන් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඉ) ෙනොඑෙසේ නම් ඒ මන්ද? உள்ᾧராட்சி, மாகாணசைபகள் அைமச்சைரக் ேகட்ட வினா: (அ) (i ) பத்ேதகம பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசத்தில் ெதாைலேபசி கம்பனிகளால் தற்ேபாᾐ ெபாᾞத்தப் பட்ᾌள்ள ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்களின் எண்ணிக்ைக மற்ᾠம் அந்த இடங்களின் ᾙகவாிகள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) உாிய கம்பனிகᾦம் வᾞடᾙம் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா? (ஆ) (i ) இந்த கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்குாியதாக ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யேவண்ᾊய நிபந்தைனகள் யாைவெயன்ப ைதᾜம், ( i i ) இதன்ேபாᾐ உாிய ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பனிகள், ஒவ்ெவாᾞ இடத்திற்கும் தனித்தனியாக உாிய நிபந்தைனகைள ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்ᾐள்ளனவா என்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்குச் சமர்ப்பிப்பாரா? (இ) உாிய நிபந்தைனகள் ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யப்படாத நிைலயில், ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்கு உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனம் அங்கீகாரம் வழங்கியிᾞந்தால் அᾐ ஒᾞ குற்றமாகும் என்பைத அவர் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்வாரா? (ஈ)(i ) ஆெமனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், (ii) கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐம்ேபாᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடக்க ேவண்ᾊய பணᾙம் கிைடத்ᾐள்ள பணᾙம் ெவவ்ேவறாக எவ்வள ெவன்பைதᾜம், (iii) உாிய பணத்ெதாைக கிைடக்கவில்ைலெயனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், (iv) உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடத்த ேமற்பᾊ பணத்ெதாைக எந்த நடவᾊக்ைககᾦக்காக ெசலவிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ என்பைதᾜம் அவர் குறிப்பிᾌவாரா? (b) Will he submit to this House- (i) the conditions that have to be fulfilled with regard to the installation of these towers; and (ii) whether the relevant conditions have been fulfilled separately as per each location by the relevant telephone companies?

(e) Does not arise. ඇමුණුම 01 இைணப்ᾗ 01 Annex 01 1. Sharing of Antenna Structures 1.1 Antenna structures should be used on sharing basis for which the tariff schedule will be determined by TRCSL in consultation with the TISPs. The minimum number of antenna structures that conform to the technical requirements will be approved for an identified Antenna Structure Farm. 1.2 The TRCSL will initiate the formation of a new Antenna Structure Farm when the necessity arises. TISPs may propose such locations to TRCSL. 1.3 The antenna structure shall be designed and constructed to accommodate a minimum of 20 square meters of additional design antenna area (from the top portion) for at least two other TSPs. Physical space required for fixing of the additional antenna shall be reserved at top portion. This allocation of additional design antenna area will be encouraged through incentive schemes. 1.4 Initially up to three requests will be considered to construct separate antenna structures within the Antenna Structure Farm. Subsequent applicants should share one of the available antenna structures. Applications for additional antenna structures will be considered only under special circumstances and such applications will be referred to the TAC with justification for such request. 1.5 The Antenna Structure Farm will be confined to a minimum feasible area by the TRCSL, subject to a maximum radius of 250 m. 1.6 The distance between Antenna Structure Farms will be kept at a minimum separation of 4 km. 1.7 Both TSPs and TISPs may obtain approval to erect roof top masts of height not exceeding 20 meters from the roof top within or in between Antenna Structure Farms. 1.8 Broadcasting antenna structures are exempted from the clauses 1.3 and 1.4 provided that application is initially forwarded for an Antenna Structure to be used only for broadcasting purposes. 1.9 Cumulative radio frequency power density due to Antenna Structure Farm should be within the limits defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL provided that the maximum RF power levels allowed are as per Annexure I. 2. Height Clearance 2.1 Maximum height of the antenna structure shall be based on the recommendations of the CAASL, MOD and UDA.

3. Lightning Protection 3.1 The Antenna Structure premises should be provided with a comprehensive lightning protection scheme to minimize the lightning related damage and injury as per the Annexure II (a). 3.2 The antenna structure should conform to the guidelines specified in Annexure II (b) with regard to the lightning protection concerns. 3.3 installation of the lightning protection system should be carried out by the TISP as per Annexure II (b). 3.4 An insurance cover shall be in place against any lightning related damage to the neighbourhood due to the existence of the antenna structure. 3.5 A report on the lighting protection system, and other specified information as per Annexure III, shall be submitted to TRCSL by TISP twice a year. 4. Electromagnetic Interference and Health Concerns 4.1 Base Station equipment shall comply with the EMC standards acceptable to TRCSL. 4.2 TRCSL will enforce and monitor maximum RF power density criteria defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL as per Annexure I. 4.3 Verification of compliance with stipulated standards will be carried out by TRCSL or a recognized institution to ensure public safety. 5. Environmental Concerns 5.1 Natural environment of the area shall be protected from any potential adverse impacts in accordance with CEA or PEA approval. 6. Construction of Antenna Structures 6.1 The Antenna structure and other related infrastructure should be designed and constructed in conformity with BS 8100, TIA/EIA 222F (or latest) or other equivalent international standard accepted by TRCSL. 6.2 All antenna structures with heights exceeding 30m should be designed and detailed as post - disaster type structures. 6.3 All the structural designs, construction drawings and proposals are required to be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 6.4 Institutes and individuals who do the certification should be registered with TRC. 6.5 Minimum of third-party insurance coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury should be taken during the construction of antenna structure. A copy of the same should be submitted to TRCSL before commencement of the development. 6.6 During the construction, the antenna structure should be installed with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 6.7 TISPs should obtain development permits from respective Local Authorities. All the approving agencies are encouraged to establish electronic document transfer in order to expedite the approval process. 6.8 TISP who has received approval is required to complete the construction of the new antenna structure within six months

[ගරු ජනක බණ්ඩාර ෙතන්නෙකෝන් මහතා]

2010 ජනවාරි 05 2031 2032

from the date of granting the approval. Failure to meet this requirement without a valid reason acceptable to TRCSL will result in cancellation of the approval. The new antenna structure should be available for sharing within 03 months from the date of completion. 6.9 No Telecommunication Antenna Structure should be constructed without written approval of TRCSL. 7. Installation of Antenna Structures on Buildings 7.1 The structural stability of the buildings, which are primarily designed for purposes other than facilitating antenna structures, should be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design, prior to the approval for the construction of the Antenna Structure. 7.2 The TISP should obtain the planning clearance from UDA with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 7.3 Antenna structure outside the areas declared under UDA Law will be considered for approval with the consent of relevant Local Authorities. 7.4 Antenna structures less than 5m in height above roof top level are required to obtain clearance only from the MOD and CAASL. 7.5 A lightning protection system should be installed as per the Annexure II (b), to ensure the safety of occupants. 7.6 All antenna structures on buildings with total height exceeding 30m above ground level should be designed and detailed as post-disaster type structures. All proposals shall be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 7.7 Installations of Antenna Structures on buildings should conform to all other Guidelines in this document. 8. Maintenance of Antenna Structures 8.1 Lighting and painting of Antenna Structures must be in accordance with the specifications of CAASL. 8.2 Antenna structure operator should submit a monthly report in electronic form to TRCSL indicating the information as per format No: TRC/NWMR - 01. 8.3 Maintenance of antenna structure shall be carried out in accordance with Annexure IV. 8.4 Maintenance of Lightning protection system should be done by the TISP in compliance with specifications given in Annexure II (c).. 9. Alteration to Antenna Structures 9.1 Upon justifiable request(s) made by concerned parties, the TRCSL, in consultation with relevant authorities, may consider removal or alteration to the structure or suspension of operation. In such see all costs should be borne by the TISP. 9.2 To ensure the safety of the public and property, an Antenna Structure should not be abandoned even for short periods of time, unless otherwise it is completely removed. The TISP should inform the TRCSL and make arrangements to either remove a non-operational installation or transfer it to another antennae structure operator. Until the antenna structure is removed or transferred and the TRCSL is informed the same, the TISP is responsible for the maintenance of the antenna structure in conformity with provisions specified.

9.3 Any structural alterations to the Antenna Structure or its supporting structure, beyond what has been envisaged in the approved design, require the certification of a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design to get the approval of the TRCSL. 9.4 Removal of an Antenna Structure also requires insurance to be taken for the coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury during the removal of antenna structure. 10. Approval Procedure 10.1 TISP should submit an application as per Annexure V in the form of soft and hard copies. 10.2 Approval Procedure is as specified in Annexure VI. 11. General 11.1 All relevant authorities such as CEA, PEA, UDA, CAASL, LA, CEB and TRCSL are required to facilitate the TISPs in establishing antenna structures to provide telecommunication services on a priority basis, as telecommunication networks are a vital component of infrastructure development while addressing the public health & safety, economic, environmental and other impacts. 11.2 Appeals for any deviation from these guidelines caused by technical or commercial issues will be referred to the TAC who will meet once in a month. යක්කලමුල්ල පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු யக்கலᾙல்ல பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் YAKKALAMULLA PRADESHIYA SABHA AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS

0555/’09 5. ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා ( மாண்ᾗமிகு அஜித் குமார) (The Hon. Ajith Kumara) පළාත් පාලන සහ පළාත් සභා අමාතɕතුමාෙගන් ඇසූ පශ්නය - (2): (අ) (i) යක්කලමුල්ල පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය තුළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් ෙම් වන විට සවි කර තිෙබන දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු සංඛɕාව හා එම ස්ථානයන්හි ලිපිනයන් කවෙර්ද; (ii) අදාළ සමාගම් හා කුලුනු සවි කළ වර්ෂයන් කවෙර්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට දන්වන්ෙනහිද? asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils:

(a) (i) 01 tower. 1. Malandeniya, Yakkalamulla. (ii) 1. Dialog Company 2006 (b) (i) Conditions stipulated by the Telecommunication Regulatory Commission are indicated in Annex 01. (ii) Yes. (c) Yes. (e) Does not arise. ඇමුණුම 01 இைணப்ᾗ 01 Annex 01 1. Sharing of Antenna Structures 1.1 Antenna structures should be used on sharing basis for which the tariff schedule will be determined by TRCSL in consultation with the TISPs. The minimum number of antenna structures that conform to the technical requirements will be approved for an identified Antenna Structure Farm. 1.2 The TRCSL will initiate the formation of a new Antenna Structure Farm when the necessity arises. TISPs may propose such locations to TRCSL. 1.3 The antenna structure shall be designed and constructed to accommodate a minimum of 20 square meters of additional design antenna area (from the top portion) for at least two other TSPs. Physical space required for fixing of the additional antenna shall be reserved at top portion. This allocation of additional design antenna area will be encouraged through incentive schemes. 1.4 Initially up to three requests will be considered to construct separate antenna structures within the Antenna Structure Farm. Subsequent applicants should share one of the available

antenna structures. Applications for additional antenna structures will be considered only under special circumstances and such applications will be referred to the TAC with justification for such request. 1.5 The Antenna Structure Farm will be confined to a minimum feasible area by the TRCSL, subject to a maximum radius of 250 m. 1.6 The distance between Antenna Structure Farms will be kept at a minimum separation of 4 km. 1.7 Both TSPs and TISPs may obtain approval to erect roof top masts of height not exceeding 20 meters from the roof top within or in between Antenna Structure Farms. 1.8 Broadcasting antenna structures are exempted from the clauses 1.3 and 1.4 provided that application is initially forwarded for an Antenna Structure to be used only for broadcasting purposes. 1.9 Cumulative radio frequency power density due to Antenna Structure Farm should be within the limits defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL provided that the maximum RF power levels allowed are as per Annexure I. 2. Height Clearance 2.1 Maximum height of the antenna structure shall be based on the recommendations of the CAASL, MOD and UDA.

Lightning Protection 3.1 The Antenna Structure premises should be provided with a comprehensive lightning protection scheme to minimize the lightning related damage and injury as per the Annexure II (a). 3.2 The antenna structure should conform to the guidelines specified in Annexure II (b) with regard to the lightning protection concerns. 3.3 installation of the lightning protection system should be carried out by the TISP as per Annexure II (b). 3.4 An insurance cover shall be in place against any lightning related damage to the neighbourhood due to the existence of the antenna structure. 3.5 A report on the lighting protection system, and other specified information as per Annexure III, shall be submitted to TRCSL by TISP twice a year. 4. Electromagnetic Interference and Health Concerns 4.1 Base Station equipment shall comply with the EMC standards acceptable to TRCSL. 4.2 TRCSL will enforce and monitor maximum RF power density criteria defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL as per Annexure I. 4.3 Verification of compliance with stipulated standards will be carried out by TRCSL or a recognized institution to ensure public safety. 5. Environmental Concerns 5.1 Natural environment of the area shall be protected from any potential adverse impacts in accordance with CEA or PEA approval.

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2037 2038

6. Construction of Antenna Structures 6.1 The Antenna structure and other related infrastructure should be designed and constructed in conformity with BS 8100, TIA/EIA 222F (or latest) or other equivalent international standard accepted by TRCSL. 6.2 All antenna structures with heights exceeding 30m should be designed and detailed as post - disaster type structures. 6.3 All the structural designs, construction drawings and proposals are required to be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 6.4 Institutes and individuals who do the certification should be registered with TRC. 6.5 Minimum of third-party insurance coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury should be taken during the construction of antenna structure. A copy of the same should be submitted to TRCSL before commencement of the development. 6.6 During the construction, the antenna structure should be installed with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 6.7 TISPs should obtain development permits from respective Local Authorities. All the approving agencies are encouraged to establish electronic document transfer in order to expedite the approval process. 6.8 TISP who has received approval is required to complete the construction of the new antenna structure within six months from the date of granting the approval. Failure to meet this requirement without a valid reason acceptable to TRCSL will result in cancellation of the approval. The new antenna structure should be available for sharing within 03 months from the date of completion. 6.9 No Telecommunication Antenna Structure should be constructed without written approval of TRCSL. 7. Installation of Antenna Structures on Buildings 7.1 The structural stability of the buildings, which are primarily designed for purposes other than facilitating antenna structures, should be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design, prior to the approval for the construction of the Antenna Structure. 7.2 The TISP should obtain the planning clearance from UDA with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 7.3 Antenna structure outside the areas declared under UDA Law will be considered for approval with the consent of relevant Local Authorities. 7.4 Antenna structures less than 5m in height above roof top level are required to obtain clearance only from the MOD and CAASL. 7.5 A lightning protection system should be installed as per the Annexure II (b), to ensure the safety of occupants. 7.6 All antenna structures on buildings with total height exceeding 30m above ground level should be designed and detailed as post-disaster type structures. All proposals shall be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design.

7.7 Installations of Antenna Structures on buildings should conform to all other Guidelines in this document. 8. Maintenance of Antenna Structures 8.1 Lighting and painting of Antenna Structures must be in accordance with the specifications of CAASL. 8.2 Antenna structure operator should submit a monthly report in electronic form to TRCSL indicating the information as per format No: TRC/NWMR - 01. 8.3 Maintenance of antenna structure shall be carried out in accordance with Annexure IV. 8.4 Maintenance of Lightning protection system should be done by the TISP in compliance with specifications given in Annexure II (c).. 9. Alteration to Antenna Structures 9.1 Upon justifiable request(s) made by concerned parties, the TRCSL, in consultation with relevant authorities, may consider removal or alteration to the structure or suspension of operation. In such see all costs should be borne by the TISP. 9.2 To ensure the safety of the public and property, an Antenna Structure should not be abandoned even for short periods of time, unless otherwise it is completely removed. The TISP should inform the TRCSL and make arrangements to either remove a non-operational installation or transfer it to another antennae structure operator. Until the antenna structure is removed or transferred and the TRCSL is informed the same, the TISP is responsible for the maintenance of the antenna structure in conformity with provisions specified. 9.3 Any structural alterations to the Antenna Structure or its supporting structure, beyond what has been envisaged in the approved design, require the certification of a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design to get the approval of the TRCSL. 9.4 Removal of an Antenna Structure also requires insurance to be taken for the coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury during the removal of antenna structure. 10. Approval Procedure 10.1 TISP should submit an application as per Annexure V in the form of soft and hard copies. 10.2 Approval Procedure is as specified in Annexure VI. 11. General 11.1 All relevant authorities such as CEA, PEA, UDA, CAASL, LA, CEB and TRCSL are required to facilitate the TISPs in establishing antenna structures to provide telecommunication services on a priority basis, as telecommunication networks are a vital component of infrastructure development while addressing the public health & safety, economic, environmental and other impacts. 11.2 Appeals for any deviation from these guidelines caused by technical or commercial issues will be referred to the TAC who will meet once in a month.

[ගරු ජනක බණ්ඩාර ෙතන්නෙකෝන් මහතා]

2010 ජනවාරි 05 2039 2040

නියාගම පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු நியாகம பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் NIYAGAMA PRADESHIYA SABHA AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS

0556/’09 6. ගරු අජිත් කුමාර මහතා ( மாண்ᾗமிகு அஜித் குமார) (The Hon. Ajith Kumara) පළාත් පාලන සහ පළාත් සභා අමාතɕතුමාෙගන් ඇසූ පශ්නය- (2) : (අ) (i) නියාගම පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය තුළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් ෙම් වන විට සවි කර තිෙබන දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු සංඛɕාව හා එම ස්ථානයන්හි ලිපිනයන් කවෙර්ද; (ii) අදාළ සමාගම් හා කුලුනු සවි කළ වර්ෂයන් කවෙර්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට දන්වන්ෙනහිද? (ආ) (i) එම කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට අදාළව ඉටු කළ යුතු ෙකොන්ෙද්සි කවෙර්ද; (ii) ෙමහිදී අදාළ දුරකථන සමාගම් විසින් එක් එක් ස්ථාන සඳහා අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා තිෙබ්ද; යන්න එතුමා ෙමම සභාවට ඉදිරිපත් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඇ) අදාළ ෙකොන්ෙද්සි සපුරා ෙනොමැති විට, දුරකථන කුලුනු සවි කිරීමට පළාත් පාලන ආයතනය අනුමතිය දී ඇත්නම් එය වරදක් බව එතුමා පිළිගන්ෙනහිද? (ඈ) (i) එෙසේ නම් ඒ සම්බන්ධව ගනු ලබන කියා මාර්ගය කවෙර්ද; (ii) කුලුනු සවි කිරීෙම්දී පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ලැබිය යුතු මුදල හා ලැබී ඇති මුදල ෙවන ෙවනම ෙකොපමණද; (iii) අදාළ මුදල් ලැබී ෙනොමැති නම්ඒ සම්බන්ධෙයන් ගනු ලබන කියාමාර්ගය කවෙර්ද; (iv) පළාත් පාලන ආයතනයට ෙමෙතක් ලැබී ඇති ඉහත මුදල් වැය කර ඇත්ෙත් කවර කටයුතු සඳහා ද; යන්න එතුමා සඳහන් කරන්ෙනහිද? (ඉ) ෙනොඑෙසේ නම් ඒ මන්ද? உள்ᾧராட்சி, மாகாணசைபகள் அைமச்சைரக் ேகட்ட வினா: ( அ)(i ) நியாகம பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசத்தில் ெதாைலேபசி கம்பனிகளால் தற்ேபாᾐ ெபாᾞத்தப் பட்ᾌள்ள ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்களின் எண்ணிக்ைக மற்ᾠம் அந்த இடங்களின் ᾙகவாிகள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) உாிய கம்பனிகᾦம் வᾞடᾙம் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா? ( ஆ)(i ) இந்த கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்குாியதாக ᾘர்த்திெசய்யேவண்ᾊய நிபந்தைனகள் யாைவ ெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) இதன்ேபாᾐ உாிய ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பனிகள், ஒவ்ெவாᾞ இடத்திற்கும் தனித்தனியாக உாிய நிபந்தைனகைள ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்ᾐள்ளனவா என்பைதᾜம் அவர் இச்சைபக்குச் சமர்ப்பிப்பாரா?

(இ) உாிய நிபந்தைனகள் ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யப்படாத நிைலயில், ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்கு உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனம் அங்கீகாரம் வழங்கியிᾞந்தால் அᾐ ஒᾞ குற்றமாகும் என்பைத அவர் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்வாரா? (ஈ)(i ) ஆெமனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i i ) கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐம்ேபாᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடக்க ேவண்ᾊய பணᾙம் கிைடத்ᾐள்ள பணᾙம் ெவவ்ேவறாக எவ்வள ெவன்பைதᾜம், ( i ii ) உாிய பணத்ெதாைக கிைடக்கவில்ைலெயனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம், ( i v ) உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடத்த ேமற்பᾊ பணத்ெதாைக எந்த நடவᾊக்ைககᾦக்காக ெசலவிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ என்பைதᾜம் அவர் குறிப்பிᾌவாரா? (உ) இன்ேறல், ஏன்?

asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils: (a) Will he inform this House of- (i) the number of telephone communication towers installed by telephone companies in the Niyagama Pradeshiya Sabha area and the addresses of their locations; and (ii) the relevant companies and the year? (b) Will he submit to this House- (i) the conditions that have to be fulfilled with regard to the installation of these towers; and (ii) whether the relevant conditions have been fulfilled separately as per each location by the relevant telephone companies? (c) Will he admit that it is an offence, if the local government authority had given permission to install telephone towers when the relevant conditions have not been fulfilled? (d) Will he state- (i) if so, the measures taken in this regard; (ii) separately, the amount of money payable to the local government authority in installing the towers and the amount of money that had been received; (iii) if the relevant money had not been received, the measures that will be taken in that regard; and (iv) the purposes for which the above money received by the local government authority had been spent? (e) If not, why?

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2041 2042

ගරු ජනක බණ්ඩාර ෙතන්නෙකෝන් මහතා (மாண்ᾗமிகு ஜனக பண்டார ெதன்னக்ேகான்) (The Hon. Janaka Bandara Tennakoon) (අ) (i) කුලුනු 04යි. 1. උඩුමුල්ල ෙහේන මාර්ගය, පිටිගල. 2. ෙපොද්දිවල, මත්තක. 3. කිරිමැටිය කන්ද, තල්ගස්ෙප්. 4. උඩුමුල්ල ෙහේන මාර්ගය, පිටිගල. 1. ඩයෙලොග් ෙටලිෙකොම් සමාගම 2009 2. ඩයෙලොග් ෙටලිෙකොම් සමාගම 2006 3. එයාර්ෙටල් සමාගම 2009 4. එයාර්ෙටල් සමාගම 2009 (ආ) (i) විදුලි සංෙද්ශ නියාමන ෙකොමිෂන් සභාව විසින් පනවා ඇති ෙකොන්ෙද්සි ඇමුණුෙමහි දක්වා ඇත. (ii) ඔව්. (ඇ) ඔව්. (ඈ) (i) එබඳු අවස්ථාවන් අනාවරණය වුවෙහොත් අදාළ නීති පතිපාදන අනුව කියාමාර්ග ගනු ලැෙබ්. (ii) ලැබිය යුතු මුදල ලැබී ඇති මුදල රු: 410,233.80 රු: 410,233.80 (iii) අදාළ ෙනොෙව්. (அ) ஆம் (i) ேகாᾗரங்கள் 04 1. உᾌᾙல்ல ேஹன ᾪதி, பிற்றிகல 2. ெபாத்திவல, மத்தக 3. கிறிவற்றிய கந்த, தல்கஸ்ேப 4. உᾌᾙலல்ல ேஹன ᾪதி, பிற்றிகல (ii) 1. டயெலாக் ெரᾢெகாம் கம்பனி 2009 2. டயெலாக் ெரᾢெகாம் கம்பனி 2006 3. எயார்ெரல் கம்பனி 2009 4. எயார்ெரல் கம்பனி 2009 (ஆ) (i) ெதாைலத்ெதாடர்ᾗகள் ஒᾨங்குபᾌத்தல் ஆைணக்குᾨவினால் விதிக்கப்பட்ᾌள்ள நிபந்தைனகள் இைணப்ᾗ இலப்பம் 01 இல குறிப்பிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளன. (a) (i) 04 towers 1. Udumulla Hena Road, Pitigala 2. Poddiwela, Mattaka 3. Kirimetiya Kanda, Thalgaspe 4. Udumulla Hena Road, Pitigala (ii) 1. Dialog Company 2009 2. Dialog Company 2006 3. Airtel Company 2009 4. Airtel Company 2009 (b) (i) Conditions stipulated by the Telecommunication Regulatory Commission are indicated in Annex 01. (ii) Yes. (c) Yes. (d) (i) If such situations are revealed, action will be taken in terns of the relevant legal provisions. (ii) Sum to be received Sum received Rs. 410,233.80 Rs. 410,233.80 (iii) Not applicable. (iv) After crediting to the common fund of the Local Authority, funds will be utilized for the functions approved under the Annual Budget Statement. (e) Does not arise. 1. Sharing of Antenna Structures 1.1 Antenna structures should be used on sharing basis for which the tariff schedule will be determined by TRCSL in consultation with the TISPs. The minimum number of antenna structures that conform to the technical requirements will be approved for an identified Antenna Structure Farm. 1.2 The TRCSL will initiate the formation of a new Antenna Structure Farm when the necessity arises. TISPs may propose such locations to TRCSL. 1.3 The antenna structure shall be designed and constructed to accommodate a minimum of 20 square meters of additional design antenna area (from the top portion) for at least two other TSPs. Physical space required for fixing of the additional antenna shall be reserved at top portion. This allocation of additional design antenna area will be encouraged through incentive schemes. 1.4 Initially up to three requests will be considered to construct separate antenna structures within the Antenna Structure Farm. Subsequent applicants should share one of the available antenna structures. Applications for additional antenna structures will be considered only under special circumstances and such applications will be referred to the TAC with justification for such request. 1.5 The Antenna Structure Farm will be confined to a minimum feasible area by the TRCSL, subject to a maximum radius of 250 m. 1.6 The distance between Antenna Structure Farms will be kept at a minimum separation of 4 km. 1.7 Both TSPs and TISPs may obtain approval to erect roof top masts of height not exceeding 20 meters from the roof top within or in between Antenna Structure Farms.

2010 ජනවාරි 05 2043 2044

1.8 Broadcasting antenna structures are exempted from the clauses 1.3 and 1.4 provided that application is initially forwarded for an Antenna Structure to be used only for broadcasting purposes. 1.9 Cumulative radio frequency power density due to Antenna Structure Farm should be within the limits defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL provided that the maximum RF power levels allowed are as per Annexure I. 2. Height Clearance 2.1 Maximum height of the antenna structure shall be based on the recommendations of the CAASL, MOD and UDA. 3. Lightning Protection 3.1 The Antenna Structure premises should be provided with a comprehensive lightning protection scheme to minimize the lightning related damage and injury as per the Annexure II (a). 3.2 The antenna structure should conform to the guidelines specified in Annexure II (b) with regard to the lightning protection concerns. 3.3 installation of the lightning protection system should be carried out by the TISP as per Annexure II (b). 3.4 An insurance cover shall be in place against any lightning related damage to the neighbourhood due to t he existence of the antenna structure. 3.5 A report on the lighting protection system, and other specified information as per Annexure III, shall be submitted to TRCSL by TISP twice a year. 4. Electromagnetic Interference and Health Concerns 4.1 Base Station equipment shall comply with the EMC standards acceptable to TRCSL. 4.2 TRCSL will enforce and monitor maximum RF power density criteria defined by ICNIRP and adopted by TRCSL as per Annexure I. 4.3 Verification of compliance with stipulated standards will be carried out by TRCSL or a recognized institution to ensure public safety. 5. Environmental Concerns 5.1 Natural environment of the area shall be protected from any potential adverse impacts in accordance with CEA or PEA approval. 6. Construction of Antenna Structures 6.1 The Antenna structure and other related infrastructure should be designed and constructed in conformity with BS 8100, TIA/EIA 222F (or latest) or other equivalent international standard accepted by TRCSL. 6.2 All antenna structures with heights exceeding 30m should be designed and detailed as post - disaster type structures. 6.3 All the structural designs, construction drawings and proposals are required to be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 6.4 Institutes and individuals who do the certification should be registered with TRC.

6.5 Minimum of third-party insurance coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury should be taken during the construction of antenna structure. A copy of the same should be submitted to TRCSL before commencement of the development. 6.6 During the construction, the antenna structure should be installed with an aircraft warning light, as per CAASL recommendations. 6.7 TISPs should obtain development permits from respective Local Authorities. All the approving agencies are encouraged to establish electronic document transfer in order to expedite the approval process. 6.8 TISP who has received approval is required to complete the construction of the new antenna structure within six months from the date of granting the approval. Failure to meet this requirement without a valid reason acceptable to TRCSL will result in cancellation of the approval. The new antenna structure should be available for sharing within 03 months from the date of completion. 6.9 No Telecommunication Antenna Structure should be constructed without written approval of TRCSL. 7. Installation of Antenna Structures on Buildings 7.1 The structural stability of the buildings, which are primarily designed for purposes other than facilitating antenna structures, should be certified by a charted civil engineer who is specialized in structural design, prior to the approval for the construction of the Antenna Structure. 7.2 The TISP should obtain the planning clearance form UDA within the areas declared under UDA Law’ 7.3 Antenna structure outside the areas declared under UDA Law will be considered for approval with the consent of relevant Local Authorities. 7.4 Antenna structures less than 5m in height above roof top level are required to obtain clearance only from the MOD and CAASL. 7.5 A lightning protection system should be installed as per the Annexure II (b), to ensure the safety of occupants. 7.6 All antenna structures on buildings with total height exceeding 30m above ground level should be designed and detailed as post-disaster type structures. All proposals shall be certified by a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design. 7.7 Installations of Antenna Structures on buildings should conform to all other Guidelines in this document. 8. Maintenance of Antenna Structures 8.1 Lighting and painting of Antenna Structures must be in accordance with the specifications of CAASL. 8.2 Antenna structure operator should submit a monthly report in electronic form to TRCSL indicating the information as per format No: TRC/NW/MR - 01. 8.3 Maintenance of antenna structure shall be carried out in accordance with Annexure IV. 8.4 Maintenance of Lightning protection system should be done by the TISP in compliance with specifications given in Annexure II (c).

පාර්ලිෙම්න්තුව 2045 2046

9. Alteration to Antenna Structures 9.1 Upon justifiable request(s) made by concerned parties, the TRCSL, in consultation with relevant authorities, may consider removal or alteration to the structure or suspension of operation. In such case all costs should be borne by the TISP. 9.2 To ensure the safety of the public and property, an Antenna Structure should not be abandoned even for short periods of time, unless otherwise it is completely removed. The TISP should inform the TRCSL and make arrangements to either remove a non-operational installation or transfer it to another antennae structure operator. Until the antenna structure is removed or transferred and the TRCSL is informed the same, the TISP is responsible for the maintenance of the antenna structure in conformity with provisions specified. 9.3 Any structural alterations to the Antenna Structure or its supporting structure, beyond what has been envisaged in the approved design, require the certification of a chartered civil engineer who is specialized in structural design to get the approval of the TRCSL. 9.4 Removal of an Antenna Structure also requires insurance to be taken for the coverage of the risk of physical damage and injury during the removal of antenna structure. 10. Approval Procedure 10.1 TISP should submit an application as per Annexure V in the form of soft and hard copies. 10.2 Approval Procedure is as specified in Annexure VI. 11. General 11.1 All relevant authorities such as CEA, PEA, UDA, CAASL, LA, CEB and TRCSL are required to facilitate the TISPs in establishing antenna structures to provide telecommunication services on a priority basis, as telecommunication networks are a vital component of infrastructure development while addressing the public health & safety, economic, environmental and other impacts. 11.2 Appeals for any deviation from these guidelines caused by technical or commercial issues will be referred to the TAC who will meet once in a month.

නාෙගොඩ පාෙද්ශීය සභා බල පෙද්ශය : දුරකථන සන්නිෙව්දන කුලුනු நாெகாட பிரேதச சைப ஆᾦைகப் பிரேதசம் : ெதாைலேபசி ெதாடர்பாடல் கம்பங்கள் NAGODA PRADESHIYA SABHA AREA : TELEPHONE COMMUNICATION TOWERS

அவர் இச்சைபக்கு அறிவிப்பாரா?

(ஆ) (i) இந்த கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்குாியதாக ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யேவண்ᾊய நிபந்தைனகள் யாைவெயன்பைத ᾜம்,

(ii) இதன்ேபாᾐ உாிய ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பனிகள், ஒவ்ெவாᾞ இடத்திற்கும் தனித்தனியாக உாிய நிபந்தைனகைள ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்ᾐள்ளனவா என்பைத ᾜம்

அவர் இச்சைபக்குச் சமர்ப்பிப்பாரா?

(இ) உாிய நிபந்தைனகள் ᾘர்த்தி ெசய்யப்படாத நிைலயில், ெதாைலேபசிக் கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐவதற்கு உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனம் அங்கீகாரம் வழங்கியிᾞந்தால் அᾐ ஒᾞ குற்றமாகும் என்பைத அவர் ஏற்ᾠக்ெகாள்வாரா?

(ஈ) (i ) ஆெமனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம்,

(ii) கம்பங்கைள ெபாᾞத்ᾐம்ேபாᾐ உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடக்க ேவண்ᾊய பணᾙம் கிைடத்ᾐள்ள பணᾙம் ெவவ்ேவறாக எவ்வள ெவன்பைதᾜம்,

(iii) உாிய பணத்ெதாைக கிைடக்கவில்ைலெயனில் அᾐ ெதாடர்பாக எᾌக்கப்பᾌம் நடவᾊக்ைககள் யாைவெயன்பைதᾜம்,

(iv) உள்ᾧராட்சி நிᾠவனத்திற்கு கிைடத்த ேமற்பᾊ பணத்ெதாைக எந்த நடவᾊக்ைககᾦக்காக ெசலவிடப்பட்ᾌள்ளᾐ என்பைதᾜம்

அவர் குறிப்பிᾌவாரா?

(உ) இன்ேறல், ஏன்?

asked the Minister of Local Government and Provincial Councils : (a) Will he inform this House of- (i) the number of telephone communication towers installed by telephone companies in the Nagoda Pradeshiya Sabha area and the addresses of their locations; and (ii) the relevant companies and the year? (b) Will he submit to this House- (i) the conditions that have to be fulfilled with regard to the installation of these towers; and (ii) whether the relevant conditions have been fulfilled separately as per each location by the relevant telephone companies?
